 kaan ko lekar kisi bhi tarah kaa jokhim uthaanaa baari pad saktaa he
 Ear khont is also known as cerumen
 yah jail jaisaa lubricant hota he jo ded cells se bana hota he
 Apart from this, it also contains fat and fine hair
 haalanki year vaix kaanon kii suraksha ke liye hote hai lekin jab yah bahut zyada jamaa ho jaataa he ki to sunai dena kam ho jaataa he
 Many times it is also prone to ear pain and infection
 yah yeardram ko bhi block kar detaa he

 isse kai tarah kii samasyaayein ho sakati hai

 kaan kii khont saaf karne kaa yah sabase purana tarika he

 The final match of IPL season 8 will be played between Chennai Super Kings and Mumbai Indians at Eden Gardens in Kolkata
 is muqaabala se judi das khaas baton par ek nazar- 1
 chennai or mumbai ipel final main teesri baar aamane-saamne hai
 When the two first met face-to-face in 2010, the bet was named after Chennai
 2013 main mumbai indiens champion bani thi
 2
 chennai super kings record chhathi baar final main pahunchi he
 The team became IPL champions in 2010 and 2011
 jabaki 2008, 2012 or 2013 main team upavijeta rahi thi
 3
 chennai final muqaabala jitkar teen baar ipel champion banane vaali pehali team ban sakati he
 4
 agar chennai khitaab jitati he to ipel itihaas main ye keval doosraa mauka hoga jab lig leader rahi team ipel kaa khitaab jeetegi
 In 2008, Rajasthan Royals managed to win the title after topping the league
 5
 Kolkata's Eden Gardens is hosting the IPL final for the second time
 isse pehle 2013 main yahaan ipel final muqabla khelaa gaya tha, jisamen mumbai ne chennai ko haraaya tha
 6
 chennai super kings ke salaami ballebaaz dwen smith 2015 main mumbai ke khilaaf khelenge
 In 2013, he played against Chennai as a Mumbai Indians opener
 7
 If Mumbai Indians win the title then Ricky Ponting will score a unique double
 ve mumbai indiens ke khilaadi ke taur par 2013 main champion banane vaali team main shaamil the or is vakt ve mumbai indiens team ke mukhya coach hai
 8
 agar sanyog kii baat karen to mumbai indiens ke champion banane kii sambhaavna zyada he
 Because during the last four seasons of the IPL, the same team has become the champion, who finished second in the league table
 is baar mumbai indiens kii team lig main duusare sthaan par rahi he
 By the way, if Mumbai Indians become champions then it will be its second title

 ipel kaa final agar barish kii vajah se nahin ho paata he to 25 may rigerv ke din ise khelaa jayega

 1
 Chennai and Mumbai are face to face for the third time in the IPL final
 2010 main jab pehali baar donon aamane-saamne hue the, tab baaji chennai ke naam rahi thi
 In 2013, Mumbai Indians became champions
 2
 Chennai Super Kings reached the final for a record sixth time
 team 2010 or 2011 main ipel champion ban chuki he
 While the team was runners-up in 2008, 2012 and 2013
 3
 Chennai can become the first team to win three times IPL champions by winning the final match
 4
 If Chennai wins the title, it will be only the second time in IPL history when the league leader will win the IPL title
 2008 main rajasthan royles lig main top rahane ke baad khitaab jeetne main kaamyaab rahi thi
 5
 kolkata kaa eden gardence duusari baar ipel final kii mejabani kar rahaa he
 Earlier in 2013, the IPL final was played here, in which Mumbai defeated Chennai

 Chennai Super Kings opener Dwayne Smith will play against Mumbai in 2015

 agar mumbai indiens kitaab jitati he to riki ponting anokhaa dabl banaaenge
